A Provisional Operational Approval is granted for the use of this Section
as set forth below.
A Provisional Operational Approval issued by CI Staff grants the save
authority, on a temporary basis, for the use of an individual as the authority
granted in en Ccernational Approval unless otherwise specified by CI/OA. It is
based, however, only on preliminary file checks and investigation and is sub-
ject to a further final review when all investigation is completed.
Subject's POA is herewith extended until 30 September 1965 to allow.
additional time for the completion of the OA investigation.
To process the Operational Approval, full Information (completed PPA
Paris I and II) must be submitted as soon as possible and not later than atx
(6) months from this date. An Operational Approval will follow when all
investigation is completed and upon the receipt of satisfactory PPA Parts i
in the U. Cancellation must be requested if use of Subject by Interested Di-
visional ceases.

PROVISIONAL OPERATIONAL APPROVAL
MEMORAROON FOR: Cate:

WH/SA/IOS - W. Ulery
148001
PICO Panan, Reinaldo
REFERENCE: Your Varenant in, Dated
22 January 1965 cma
A Provisional Operational Approval is granted for the use of this Subject
as set forth below.
A Provisional Operational Approval issued by CI Staff grants the same
authority, on a temporary basis, for the use of an individual as the authority
granted in an Operational Approval unless otherwise specified by CI/OA. It is
based, however, only on preliminary file checks and investigation and is sub-
ject to a further final review when all investigation is completed.
POA reinstated until 26 April 1965 to allow for submission of PRQ Part
I and PRQ Part II on Subject per WH/SA/IOS request of 22 January 1965.
To process the Operational Approval, full information (complete! PRQ
Parts I and I:) must be submitted us soon as possible and not later than six
(f.) months from this date. An Operational Approval will follow when all
investigation is completed and upon the receipt of satisfactory PRQ Parts I
and II. Conveliation must be requested 1 use of Subject by interested Di-
visions coverage.
Edward P. RODD
